{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Lc7QdyMzKc3PHPkG62MtvA","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01WAnMksuqGCipKJmUCNNRxx","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer API Reference Documentation\n\n## Overview\n\nThe `KafkaConsumer` is a client that consumes records from a Kafka cluster. It provides a flexible and powerful API for consuming messages from one or more topics, with support for both group-managed and manual partition assignment, automatic and manual offset management, and rich options for controlling consumption flow.\n\n### Key Characteristics\n\n- **Not Thread-Safe**: The consumer is designed for single-threaded use. All operations except `wakeup()` must be called from the same thread.\n- **Automatic Failure Handling**: Transparently handles broker failures and adapts as topic partitions migrate within the cluster.\n- **Consumer Group Support**: Enables horizontal scaling through consumer groups with automatic rebalancing.\n- **Flexible Offset Management**: Supports both automatic and manual offset commits, with optional external offset storage.\n- **TCP Connection Management**: Maintains connections to brokers; must be closed to avoid resource leaks.\n\n### Version Compatibility\n\nThe KafkaConsumer can communicate with brokers version 0.10.0 and newer. Some features may not be available on older broker versions and will raise `UnsupportedVersionException`.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Core Consumer Lifecycle\n\n### 1.1 Constructor Variants\n\n#### Basic Constructor with Map\n```java\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)\n```\nInstantiates a consumer with configuration properties. The `key.deserializer` and `value.deserializer` must be specified in the configuration.\n\n#### Constructor with Properties\n```java\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties)\n```\nInstantiates a consumer using a `Properties` object. Deserializers must be configured via properties.\n\n#### Constructor with Properties and Deserializers\n```java\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties, Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer, Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\nInstantiates a consumer with explicit deserializer instances. The `configure()` method is not called on deserializers passed directly.\n\n#### Constructor with Map and Deserializers\n```java\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs, Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer, Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\nInstantiates a consumer with configuration map and explicit deserializers.\n\n**Important**: Always call `close()` after use to release broker connections and other resources. Failure to do so will cause connection leaks.\n\n### 1.2 Resource Cleanup\n\n#### `close()`\n```java\nvoid close()\n```\nCloses the consumer with default 30-second timeout and `DEFAULT` leave group behavior. Commits offsets if auto-commit is enabled. Attempts all shutdown steps even if some fail, logging errors and throwing the first error encountered.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Flushes any pending offset commits\n- Leaves the consumer group (if group protocol is used)\n- Closes broker connections\n- Does not throw `WakeupException` from `wakeup()`\n\n#### `close(Duration timeout)`\n```java\nvoid close(Duration timeout)\n```\n**Deprecated since Kafka 4.1**: Use `close(CloseOptions)` instead.\n\nCloses the consumer with specified timeout and default leave group behavior.\n\n**Timeout Semantics**:\n- Bounds time for offset commits and group coordination\n- Actual broker operation timeout bounded by `request.timeout.ms`\n- Callback execution time (e.g., rebalance listeners) does not count against timeout\n\n#### `close(CloseOptions option)`\n```java\nvoid close(CloseOptions option)\n```\nCloses the consumer with fine-grained control over timeout and leave group behavior through `CloseOptions`.\n\n**Available Options**:\n- `timeout`: Maximum wait time (default: 30 seconds)\n- `leaveGroup`: Controls whether to leave the consumer group (SKIP, DEFAULT, or ASYNC)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Subscription and Assignment Models\n\nKafka offers two mutually exclusive models for partition assignment: **dynamic subscription** (group-managed) and **manual assignment**.\n\n### 2.1 Dynamic Subscription (Group-Managed)\n\nIn this model, the consumer group coordinator automatically assigns partitions to consumers. Partitions are rebalanced whenever group membership or topic metadata changes.\n\n#### `subscribe(Collection<String> topics)`\n```java\nvoid subscribe(Collection<String> topics)\n```\nSubscribe to a list of topics with no rebalance listener.\n\n**Parameters**:\n- `topics`: Non-null, non-empty list of topics (empty list treated as `unsubscribe()`)\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Replaces previous subscription/assignment\n- Uses no-op rebalance listener (all callbacks are ignored)\n- If you need custom rebalance handling, use `subscribe(Collection<String>, ConsumerRebalanceListener)`\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If topics is null, contains null/empty elements\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `assign()` was previously called, or `subscribe(Pattern)` is active, or no partition assignor configured\n\n#### `subscribe(Collection<String> topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)`\n```java\nvoid subscribe(Collection<String> topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\n```\nSubscribe to topics with explicit rebalance callbacks.\n\n**Rebalance Callback Execution**:\n- Callbacks execute only during `poll()` calls\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` called BEFORE partitions reassigned\n- `onPartitionsAssigned()` called AFTER rebalance completes (even with zero new partitions)\n- Callback exceptions propagate to the current `poll()` call\n\n**Rebalance Triggers**:\n- Consumer group membership changes (join/leave/failure)\n- Topic partition count changes\n- New topics matching subscription created\n- Topic metadata refresh shows new partitions\n\n#### Pattern Subscription: `subscribe(Pattern pattern)`\n```java\nvoid subscribe(Pattern pattern)\n```\nSubscribe to all topics matching a regex pattern.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Pattern matching occurs periodically against existing topics\n- Frequency controlled by `metadata.max.age.ms`\n- Partitions of matching topics dynamically assigned/unassigned\n- New topics created after subscription start matching if they match pattern\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If pattern is null\n- `IllegalStateException`: If assignment/other subscription model active\n\n#### Pattern Subscription with Listener\n```java\nvoid subscribe(Pattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\n```\nPattern subscription with custom rebalance handling.\n\n#### Subscription Pattern with Google RE2/J: `subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern)`\n```java\nvoid subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern)\nvoid subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\n```\nAdvanced pattern subscription supporting Google RE2/J regex syntax. **Only supported under CONSUMER group protocol**.\n\n**Validation**:\n- Incompatible patterns raise `InvalidRegularExpression` on next `poll()`\n\n#### `unsubscribe()`\n```java\nvoid unsubscribe()\n```\nClears all topic subscriptions and manual assignments.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Revokes all currently assigned partitions\n- Clears both dynamic subscriptions and manual assignments\n- No rebalance triggered\n- Position is reset; next assignment starts from committed/default offsets\n\n### 2.2 Manual Partition Assignment\n\nIn this model, the application explicitly specifies which partitions to consume. No group coordination or rebalancing occurs.\n\n#### `assign(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nvoid assign(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nManually assign a list of partitions to this consumer.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Replaces previous assignment\n- Empty assignment treated as `unsubscribe()`\n- No consumer group coordination (no rebalancing)\n- Offsets committed to group using configured `group.id`, but group membership not maintained\n- Each consumer acts independently; ensure unique `group.id` to avoid offset conflicts\n\n**Advantages**:\n- Deterministic partition assignment\n- No rebalancing overhead\n- Suitable for applications managing own state per partition\n\n**Disadvantages**:\n- No automatic failure recovery\n- Manual handling of topology changes\n- Difficult with dynamic partition counts\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If partitions contain null or empty topics\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `subscribe()` is active\n\n### 2.3 Assignment and Subscription Queries\n\n#### `assignment()`\n```java\nSet<TopicPartition> assignment()\n```\nReturns currently assigned partitions.\n\n**Return Value**:\n- For manual assignment: exact partitions assigned via `assign()`\n- For subscription: current assigned partitions (may be empty if no rebalance yet, or reassignment in progress)\n\n#### `subscription()`\n```java\nSet<String> subscription()\n```\nReturns currently subscribed topics.\n\n**Return Value**:\n- Empty set if no subscription active\n- Set of topics from last `subscribe()` call\n- Empty set after `unsubscribe()`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Polling and Data Fetching\n\nThe `poll()` method is the primary API for retrieving records and driving consumer group operations. It is **not a simple fetch operation**—it also executes rebalance callbacks, heartbeats, and other background work.\n\n### 3.1 Poll Method\n\n#### `poll(Duration timeout)`\n```java\nConsumerRecords<K, V> poll(final Duration timeout)\n```\nFetches records for subscribed topics or assigned partitions.\n\n**Timeout Semantics** (Important):\n- If data is immediately available, returns immediately (timeout is ignored)\n- If position advances past control records/aborted transactions in `read_committed` isolation, returns immediately\n- Otherwise, blocks up to `timeout` waiting for data\n- **Rebalances block longer than timeout**: If a rebalance starts, `poll()` will block for the full rebalance duration even if exceeds timeout\n- Poll timeout is separate from broker operation timeouts (controlled by `default.api.timeout.ms`)\n\n**Return Value**:\n- `ConsumerRecords<K, V>`: May be empty (timeout expired, no data)\n- Records organized by partition with offsets, timestamps, headers\n- `ConsumerRecords.nextOffsets()` provides next positions for all partitions with records\n\n**Preconditions**:\n- At least one topic/partition must be subscribed/assigned\n- Subscription/assignment must be valid (topics must exist for group protocol users)\n\n**Poll Loop Requirements** (Essential):\n- Call `poll()` frequently to:\n  - Send heartbeats (prevents session timeout)\n  - Detect group membership changes\n  - Execute rebalance callbacks\n  - Enforce liveness check (`max.poll.interval.ms`)\n- Failure to poll frequently triggers:\n  - Session timeout (default 10 seconds) → rebalance\n  - Liveness timeout (`max.poll.interval.ms`, default 5 minutes) → proactive group leave\n\n**Record Processing**:\n- Records may have gaps in offsets (transaction markers, aborted messages filtered in `read_committed`)\n- Transaction markers and aborted messages never returned to application\n- Key and value may be null\n- Headers always present (possibly empty)\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: Offset undefined/out-of-range with no auto-reset policy\n- `WakeupException`: If `wakeup()` called before/during poll\n- `InterruptException`: If thread interrupted\n- `AuthenticationException`: Authentication failed\n- `AuthorizationException`: Insufficient permissions\n- `KafkaException`: Unrecoverable errors (invalid group ID, session timeout, deserialization failures, rebalance callback exceptions)\n- `InvalidTopicException`: Invalid topic in current subscription\n- `UnsupportedVersionException`: Broker doesn't support requested features\n- `FencedInstanceIdException`: Consumer instance fenced by broker\n\n**Important Pattern**:\n```java\ntry {\n    while (!closed.get()) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            process(record);\n            // DO NOT commit here - wait until batch complete\n        }\n        // Commit after processing batch\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2 Record Container: ConsumerRecords\n\n#### Iterating Records\n```java\n// Iterate all records across partitions\nfor (ConsumerRecord<K, V> record : records) {\n    // Process record\n}\n\n// Iterate records for specific topic\nfor (ConsumerRecord<K, V> record : records.records(\"topic-name\")) {\n    // Process\n}\n\n// Get records for specific partition\nList<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n\n// Get all partitions with data\nSet<TopicPartition> partitions = records.partitions();\n```\n\n#### Next Offsets\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsets = records.nextOffsets();\n// Use for commitSync/commitAsync to commit next positions\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Offset Management\n\nOffsets represent positions in partitions. Kafka supports several offset concepts:\n- **Position (Current)**: Next offset to fetch (`position()`)\n- **Committed**: Last offset persisted to offset store (`committed()`)\n- **Log Start**: Earliest available offset (`beginningOffsets()`)\n- **Log End (High Water Mark)**: Latest available offset (`endOffsets()`)\n- **Last Stable Offset (LSO)**: Highest offset readable in `read_committed` mode\n\n**Key Principle**: Committed offset should always be the offset of the next message to consume, not the last consumed message.\n\n### 4.1 Automatic Offset Commits\n\nWhen `enable.auto.commit=true` (default):\n- Commits current position to offset storage periodically\n- Frequency: `auto.commit.interval.ms` (default 5 seconds)\n- Timing: After `poll()` returns (processed records may not be persisted yet!)\n- No callback or error indication\n\n**Risk**: If processing a `poll()` result fails, auto-commit proceeds anyway → message loss\n\n**When to Use**: Simple scenarios with fault-tolerant downstream or acceptable loss.\n\n### 4.2 Manual Synchronous Commits\n\n#### `commitSync()`\n```java\nvoid commitSync()\n```\nCommits the current position for all subscribed/assigned partitions.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Synchronous: blocks until success or unrecoverable error\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Commits **current position** (next offset to fetch)\n- Suitable for at-least-once semantics\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nconsumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n// Process records...\nconsumer.commitSync(); // Blocks until committed\n```\n\n#### `commitSync(Duration timeout)`\n```java\nvoid commitSync(Duration timeout)\n```\nCommits current position with explicit timeout.\n\n#### `commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets)`\n```java\nvoid commitSync(final Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets)\n```\nCommits specified offsets for specific partitions.\n\n**Parameters**:\n- `offsets`: Map from partition to offset and metadata\n- Offset should be next record to consume (e.g., `lastConsumed.offset() + 1`)\n- Can obtain from `ConsumerRecords.nextOffsets()`\n- Metadata may include leader epoch\n\n**Usage Example**:\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n        process(record);\n    }\n    // Commit offset of next record to read\n    long nextOffset = records.records(partition).get(0).offset() + partitionRecords.size();\n    consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n        partition,\n        new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset, records.nextOffsets().get(partition).metadata())\n    ));\n}\n```\n\n#### `commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nvoid commitSync(final Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, final Duration timeout)\n```\nCommits specified offsets with explicit timeout.\n\n**Exceptions from Commit**:\n- `CommitFailedException`: Partitions no longer assigned (group protocol user fenced)\n- `RebalanceInProgressException`: Rebalance in progress, positions may change\n- `WakeupException`: `wakeup()` called\n- `InterruptException`: Thread interrupted\n- `TimeoutException`: Timeout expired\n- `AuthenticationException`: Auth failed\n- `AuthorizationException`: Insufficient permissions\n\n### 4.3 Manual Asynchronous Commits\n\n#### `commitAsync()`\n```java\nvoid commitAsync()\n```\nAsynchronously commits current position. Equivalent to `commitAsync(null)`.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Non-blocking: returns immediately\n- Errors not reported (discarded unless callback provided)\n- Ordered: multiple commits sent in order\n- Guaranteed to complete before next `commitSync()` call\n\n#### `commitAsync(OffsetCommitCallback callback)`\n```java\nvoid commitAsync(OffsetCommitCallback callback)\n```\nAsynchronously commits with callback notification.\n\n**Callback Execution**:\n- Invoked when commit completes (success or failure)\n- Order: callbacks invoked in same order as `commitAsync()` calls\n- Execution: in background without blocking poll thread\n- Exception handling: callback receives exception, not thrown to caller\n\n**Callback Interface**:\n```java\n@FunctionalInterface\npublic interface OffsetCommitCallback {\n    void onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Exception exception);\n}\n```\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nconsumer.commitAsync((offsets, exception) -> {\n    if (exception != null) {\n        logger.error(\"Async commit failed\", exception);\n    }\n});\n```\n\n#### `commitAsync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, OffsetCommitCallback callback)`\n```java\nvoid commitAsync(final Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, OffsetCommitCallback callback)\n```\nAsynchronously commits specified offsets with callback.\n\n### 4.4 Querying Offsets\n\n#### `position(TopicPartition partition)`\n```java\nlong position(TopicPartition partition)\n```\nReturns the **current position** (next offset to fetch) for a partition.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Synchronous blocking call\n- May issue remote call if position undefined\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Returns offset of next record to be fetched\n\n**Postcondition**:\n- `position(partition) == committed(partition).offset() + 1` (after no consume)\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalStateException`: Partition not assigned\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: No position defined\n- `TimeoutException`: Timeout expired\n- `WakeupException`: Wakeup called\n\n#### `position(TopicPartition partition, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nlong position(TopicPartition partition, final Duration timeout)\n```\nPosition query with explicit timeout.\n\n#### `committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(final Set<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nReturns **last committed offsets** for specified partitions.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Synchronous remote call to offset coordinator\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Returns only partitions with commits; others map to null\n- Offset is \"next to read\" (last consumed + 1)\n- Metadata includes leader epoch if available\n\n**Return Value**:\n- Map with entries only for partitions with commits\n- null for partitions with no commit history\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed = consumer.committed(partitions);\nfor (TopicPartition tp : partitions) {\n    OffsetAndMetadata om = committed.get(tp);\n    if (om != null) {\n        System.out.println(\"Committed offset: \" + om.offset());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### `committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(final Set<TopicPartition> partitions, final Duration timeout)\n```\nCommitted offsets with explicit timeout.\n\n#### `beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nReturns the **earliest available offsets** for specified partitions.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Does not change consumer position\n- Remote call required; blocks until complete\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Partitions not required to be assigned\n\n**Return Value**:\n- Map of earliest available offsets per partition\n- Empty map if timeout is zero\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> offsets = consumer.beginningOffsets(partitions);\nfor (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, Long> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n    System.out.println(entry.getKey() + \" starts at \" + entry.getValue());\n}\n```\n\n#### `beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)\n```\nBeginning offsets with explicit timeout.\n\n#### `endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nReturns the **latest available offsets** for specified partitions.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- In `read_uncommitted`: high watermark (HWM)\n- In `read_committed`: Last Stable Offset (LSO) = min(HWM, first offset in open transaction)\n- Does not change position\n- Remote call; blocks until complete\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n\n**Semantics**:\n- Offset X returned means: record at offset X-1 is readable, offset X not readable yet\n- Empty partition has end offset 0\n\n#### `endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)\n```\nEnd offsets with explicit timeout.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Position Control and Seeking\n\n### 5.1 Seeking\n\nSeeking changes the position to a specific offset. Useful for replaying messages, skipping to latest, or restoring from external state.\n\n#### `seek(TopicPartition partition, long offset)`\n```java\nvoid seek(TopicPartition partition, long offset)\n```\nSeeks to specified offset.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Sets position for next `poll()`; does not affect in-flight fetches\n- Valid offsets: 0 to log end offset (or last offset for empty partitions)\n- Invalid offsets (out of range): behavior depends on `auto.offset.reset`\n  - \"earliest\": seek to start\n  - \"latest\": seek to end\n  - \"none\": `OffsetOutOfRangeException` on next poll\n\n**Important**:\n- Seek won't affect fetches already in flight\n- Consumer may wait up to `fetch.max.wait.ms` for next fetch\n- Position advances through poll; seek only changes fetch offset\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: Offset < 0\n- `IllegalStateException`: Partition not assigned\n\n#### `seek(TopicPartition partition, OffsetAndMetadata offsetAndMetadata)`\n```java\nvoid seek(TopicPartition partition, OffsetAndMetadata offsetAndMetadata)\n```\nSeeks to specified offset with metadata (including leader epoch).\n\n### 5.2 Seek-to-Position Helpers\n\n#### `seekToBeginning(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nvoid seekToBeginning(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nSeeks to earliest available offset for each partition.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Lazy evaluation: actual seek happens on next `poll()` or `position()` call\n- Empty partition set: seeks all currently assigned partitions\n- Equivalent to `seek(partition, 0)` if earliest offset is 0\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: partitions is null\n- `IllegalStateException`: Any partition not assigned\n\n#### `seekToEnd(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nvoid seekToEnd(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nSeeks to latest offset for each partition.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- `read_uncommitted`: seeks to high watermark\n- `read_committed`: seeks to Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Lazy evaluation: actual seek on next `poll()` or `position()`\n- Empty partition set: seeks all currently assigned partitions\n\n**Use Cases**:\n- Skip historical data on startup\n- Process only new messages\n\n### 5.3 Timestamp-based Seeking\n\n#### `offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch)\n```\nFinds offsets for specified timestamps.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Returns earliest offset with timestamp ≥ target timestamp\n- Remote call; blocks until complete\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Partitions not required to be assigned\n- Old message formats without timestamps return null\n\n**Return Value**:\n- Map of partition → OffsetAndTimestamp\n- null for partitions without result (no timestamp, old format)\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestamps = partitions.stream()\n    .collect(Collectors.toMap(tp -> tp, tp -> System.currentTimeMillis() - 3600000)); // 1 hour ago\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestamps);\nfor (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n    if (entry.getValue() != null) {\n        consumer.seek(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().offset());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### `offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch, Duration timeout)\n```\nOffset lookup with explicit timeout.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Flow Control and Pause/Resume\n\n### 6.1 Pause and Resume\n\nControl which partitions are fetched without unsubscribing.\n\n#### `pause(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nvoid pause(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nPauses fetching from specified partitions.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Paused partitions not returned from future `poll()` calls\n- Subscription/assignment unchanged\n- No rebalance triggered\n- Idempotent: pausing already-paused partition is no-op\n\n**Use Cases**:\n- Decouple consumption from processing (pause until workers ready)\n- Flow control in multi-partition scenarios\n- Temporarily stop processing from slow partitions\n\n**Important**: Pause state is **not preserved across rebalances**. Must re-pause in `onPartitionsAssigned()` if needed.\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalStateException`: Any partition not assigned\n\n#### `resume(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n```java\nvoid resume(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\nResumes fetching from paused partitions.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Paused partitions will be fetched in next `poll()`\n- Idempotent: resuming non-paused partition is no-op\n- Subscription unchanged\n\n#### `paused()`\n```java\nSet<TopicPartition> paused()\n```\nReturns currently paused partitions.\n\n**Return Value**: Set of TopicPartition objects; empty set if none paused\n\n### 6.2 Common Pause/Resume Pattern\n\n**Multi-threaded Processing with Worker Pool**:\n```java\nExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(10);\nQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue = new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(100);\n\n// Consumption thread\nThread consumeThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    try {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n        while (running) {\n            // If queue full, pause to avoid unbounded memory\n            if (queue.size() >= 100) {\n                consumer.pause(consumer.assignment());\n            } else {\n                consumer.resume(consumer.assignment());\n            }\n\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                queue.put(record);\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        consumer.close();\n    }\n});\n\n// Worker threads process from queue\nfor (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {\n    executor.execute(() -> {\n        try {\n            while (running) {\n                ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = queue.poll(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n                if (record != null) {\n                    process(record);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n    });\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Consumer Group Mechanics and Rebalancing\n\nConsumer groups enable horizontal scaling by distributing partitions across multiple consumers. The broker coordinates group membership and rebalancing.\n\n### 7.1 Group Membership and Heartbeats\n\n**Session Timeout** (`session.timeout.ms`, default 10s):\n- Broker expects heartbeat at least every `session.timeout.ms`\n- If heartbeat not received, consumer considered dead\n- Partitions reassigned to other consumers\n- Triggered when `poll()` not called for duration\n\n**Poll Interval Timeout** (`max.poll.interval.ms`, default 5 minutes):\n- Consumer must call `poll()` at least every `max.poll.interval.ms`\n- If exceeded, consumer **proactively leaves group**\n- Next commit will fail with `CommitFailedException`\n- Safety mechanism against livelock (consumer processing but making no progress)\n\n**Poll frequency**: Call `poll()` more frequently than `max.poll.interval.ms` to stay in group.\n\n### 7.2 ConsumerRebalanceListener Interface\n\nThe rebalance listener allows custom handling of partition assignment changes.\n\n#### Interface Definition\n```java\npublic interface ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions);\n    void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions);\n    default void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        onPartitionsRevoked(partitions);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### `onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nCalled when partitions are being revoked before reassignment.\n\n**When Called**:\n- Graceful rebalance (normal group changes)\n- Closing consumer\n- Unsubscribing\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Called BEFORE partitions reassigned\n- Single-threaded: executes in poll() thread\n- Exceptions propagate to `poll()` call\n\n**Classic Protocol with Eager Rebalancing**: All partitions revoked even if no change\n**Classic/Cooperative or Consumer Protocol**: Only changed partitions revoked\n\n**Typical Use**: Commit offsets, flush caches\n```java\n@Override\npublic void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    // Commit offsets for partitions being revoked\n    consumer.commitSync();\n    // Flush any cached state\n    cache.flush();\n}\n```\n\n#### `onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nCalled when new partitions assigned after rebalance completes.\n\n**When Called**:\n- After each rebalance (even if no new partitions)\n- Before fetching from assigned partitions\n- Single-threaded: in poll() thread\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Called with newly assigned partitions (not previously owned)\n- Guaranteed after all previous members' `onPartitionsRevoked()` completes\n- Can query/modify consumer state before fetching starts\n\n**Typical Use**: Initialize position, load state\n```java\n@Override\npublic void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n        // Load last processed offset from external store\n        long offset = stateStore.getOffset(partition);\n        consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### `onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nCalled when partitions lost unexpectedly (not gracefully revoked).\n\n**When Called**:\n- Session timeout expired\n- Fencing by broker\n- Other fatal group errors\n- Partitions already owned by other consumers (cannot commit)\n\n**Default Behavior**: Calls `onPartitionsRevoked()`\n\n**Typical Use**: Skip expensive operations (don't commit, already owned)\n```java\n@Override\npublic void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    // Don't commit - partitions owned by others\n    // Just cleanup local state\n    for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n        stateStore.clear(partition);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 7.3 Rebalance Protocols\n\nKafka supports multiple group coordination protocols:\n\n**CLASSIC (Eager Rebalancing)**:\n- All members revoke all partitions\n- Broker reassigns all partitions\n- Higher coordination overhead\n- Simple to reason about\n\n**COOPERATIVE**:\n- Only revoke partitions actually moving\n- Reduces stop-the-world effect\n- Requires stateless partition assignment\n- Modern default\n\n**CONSUMER**:\n- New group coordination protocol (4.0+)\n- More efficient rebalancing\n- Improved performance\n\n### 7.4 Enforce Rebalance\n\n#### `enforceRebalance()`\n```java\nvoid enforceRebalance()\nvoid enforceRebalance(final String reason)\n```\n\nForces a rebalance on next `poll()`.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Non-blocking; actual rebalance on next `poll()`\n- Useful when external state changes affect partition assignment\n- Assignor can use `userdata` to transmit state in rebalance\n\n**Use Case**: Stream processor detects topology change\n```java\nif (topologyChanged()) {\n    consumer.enforceRebalance(\"Topology change detected\");\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Transactional Message Consumption\n\n### 8.1 Isolation Levels\n\n**read_uncommitted** (default):\n- Reads all messages regardless of transaction status\n- Includes aborted transaction messages\n- Faster; low latency\n- Suitable for non-critical data\n\n**read_committed**:\n- Reads only committed transaction messages\n- Aborted messages filtered out\n- Control records (markers) filtered out\n- End offset is Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n\n### 8.2 Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n\nThe LSO is the highest offset safe to read in `read_committed` mode. It's the minimum of:\n- High watermark (last replicated message + 1)\n- First offset in any open transaction\n\n**Implications**:\n- `endOffsets()` returns LSO, not HWM\n- `seekToEnd()` seeks to LSO\n- Fetch may return fewer records than requested\n- Gaps in offsets due to filtered aborted messages\n\n### 8.3 Transactional Semantics\n\nWith `isolation.level=read_committed`:\n- Consumer never sees uncommitted messages from ongoing transactions\n- Consumer never sees aborted messages\n- Consistent application-level reads across partitions\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.put(ConsumerConfig.ISOLATION_LEVEL_CONFIG, \"read_committed\");\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Thread Safety and Multi-threaded Consumption\n\n### 9.1 Thread Safety Model\n\n**NOT thread-safe**:\n- All operations except `wakeup()` must be called from single thread\n- Concurrent calls cause `ConcurrentModificationException`\n- No synchronization provided by consumer\n\n**Exception**: `wakeup()` is thread-safe and can be called from any thread.\n\n### 9.2 Wakeup and Interruption\n\n#### `wakeup()`\n```java\nvoid wakeup()\n```\nWakes up consumer thread from blocking operation.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Thread-safe; call from any thread\n- If blocked in poll(), position(), etc., raises `WakeupException`\n- If no thread blocked, next blocking call raises `WakeupException`\n- Useful for graceful shutdown from different thread\n\n**Usage Pattern**:\n```java\npublic class ConsumerWorker implements Runnable {\n    private final AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n\n    public void run() {\n        try {\n            consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n            while (!closed.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    process(record);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            if (!closed.get()) {\n                throw e; // Unexpected wakeup\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void shutdown() {\n        closed.set(true);\n        consumer.wakeup(); // Wake up poll from shutdown thread\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Thread Interrupts\n\nJava thread interrupts can also wake up the consumer (raises `InterruptException`), but discouraged:\n- May cause unclean shutdown\n- `wakeup()` preferred\n- Supported for cases where `wakeup()` not possible (external thread pool)\n\n### 9.3 Multi-threaded Consumption Patterns\n\n#### Pattern 1: One Consumer Per Thread\n\nEach thread owns a separate consumer instance.\n\n**Pros**:\n- Simple; no coordination\n- Fastest (no synchronization)\n- In-order processing per partition\n- Each thread isolated\n\n**Cons**:\n- More TCP connections (one per consumer)\n- Slight increase in request overhead\n- Limited by number of partitions\n\n#### Pattern 2: Decouple Consumption and Processing\n\nSingle consumer thread feeds records to worker thread pool.\n\n**Pros**:\n- Scale workers independently of partitions\n- Resource efficient\n- Handles variable processing time\n\n**Cons**:\n- In-order processing harder\n- Manual offset management complex\n- Need thread-safe queue\n\n**Implementation**:\n```java\n// Consumer thread\nThread consumeThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    try {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n        while (!closed.get()) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                queue.put(record); // Non-blocking; blocks if queue full\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        consumer.close();\n    }\n});\n\n// Worker threads\nExecutorService workers = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(8);\nfor (int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {\n    workers.execute(() -> {\n        try {\n            while (!closed.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = queue.poll(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n                if (record != null) {\n                    process(record);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n    });\n}\n```\n\n**Offset Management**: Ensure committed offset tracks slowest worker\n```java\nConcurrentHashMap<TopicPartition, Long> minProcessedOffset = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n\n// Worker threads update when done\nminProcessedOffset.put(partition, processedOffset);\n\n// Consumption thread commits periodically\nconsumer.commitAsync((offsets, exception) -> {\n    // Handle errors\n});\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Error Handling and Recovery\n\n### 10.1 Exception Hierarchy\n\n**Recoverable Exceptions** (retry or continue):\n- `RetriableCommitFailedException`: Commit timeout; retry\n- `TimeoutException`: Operation timeout; retry\n- `WakeupException`: Expected wakeup; handle gracefully\n- `InterruptException`: Thread interrupted; cleanup\n\n**Unrecoverable Exceptions** (fatal):\n- `CommitFailedException`: Partitions fenced (no longer owned)\n- `FencedInstanceIdException`: Instance fenced by broker\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: Offset out of range, no auto-reset\n- `AuthenticationException`: Auth failed\n- `AuthorizationException`: Insufficient permissions\n- `InvalidGroupIdException`: Invalid/missing group ID\n\n**KafkaException** (parent of all):\n- Other unrecoverable errors\n- Deserialization failures\n- Invalid configuration\n- Rebalance callback exceptions\n\n### 10.2 Error Recovery Patterns\n\n**Commit Failures**:\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (RetriableCommitFailedException e) {\n    logger.warn(\"Commit retryable error; will retry on next poll\");\n    // Retry on next iteration\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Consumer fenced; exiting consumer group\");\n    // Unrecoverable; exit\n    throw new RuntimeException(e);\n} catch (TimeoutException e) {\n    logger.warn(\"Commit timeout; retrying\");\n    consumer.commitSync(); // Retry\n}\n```\n\n**Poll Failures**:\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        try {\n            process(record);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.error(\"Record processing failed; continuing\", e);\n            // Continue; don't block other records\n        }\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    logger.info(\"Consumer woke up; exiting\");\n    throw e;\n} catch (InvalidOffsetException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Invalid offset; seeking to earliest\");\n    consumer.seekToBeginning(consumer.assignment());\n    // Retry poll\n} catch (AuthorizationException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Authorization failed; exiting\");\n    throw new RuntimeException(e);\n}\n```\n\n**Deserialization Errors**:\nConfigure error handler or use error tolerance:\n```java\nprops.put(ConsumerConfig.VALUE_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n// Default: stop on deserialization error\n// To skip: use custom deserializer or error handling middleware\n```\n\n### 10.3 Log Truncation\n\n**LogTruncationException** raised when:\n- Topic log is truncated while consumer consuming\n- Committed offset becomes invalid (< log start offset)\n\n**Recovery**:\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n} catch (LogTruncationException e) {\n    // Log truncated; reset to beginning\n    for (TopicPartition tp : e.offsetOutOfRange().keySet()) {\n        consumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singletonList(tp));\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Metadata and Monitoring\n\n### 11.1 Partition and Topic Metadata\n\n#### `partitionsFor(String topic)`\n```java\nList<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic)\n```\nGets partition metadata for topic.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Remote call; blocks until complete\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Empty list if topic not found\n- Triggers metadata refresh if needed\n\n**Return Value**: List of PartitionInfo with partition id, leader, replicas, ISR\n\n#### `partitionsFor(String topic, Duration timeout)`\n```java\nList<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic, Duration timeout)\n```\nTopic partitions with explicit timeout.\n\n#### `listTopics()`\n```java\nMap<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics()\n```\nGets metadata for all authorized topics.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Remote call; blocks until complete\n- Timeout: `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Returns empty map if no topics authorized\n\n#### `listTopics(Duration timeout)`\n```java\nMap<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics(Duration timeout)\n```\nList all topics with explicit timeout.\n\n### 11.2 Consumer Group Metadata\n\n#### `groupMetadata()`\n```java\nConsumerGroupMetadata groupMetadata()\n```\nReturns metadata about consumer's group membership.\n\n**Return Value**: ConsumerGroupMetadata with generation ID, group ID, member ID\n\n**Use Cases**:\n- Passing to transactional producer\n- Coordinating with other systems\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `InvalidGroupIdException`: Consumer not in group (using manual assignment)\n\n### 11.3 Lag Monitoring\n\n#### `currentLag(TopicPartition topicPartition)`\n```java\nOptionalLong currentLag(TopicPartition topicPartition)\n```\nReturns lag (difference between end offset and position).\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Uses cached metadata; doesn't block\n- Empty if position or end offset unknown\n- Triggers metadata fetch if needed but returns immediately\n\n**Lag = endOffset - position**\n\n**Return Value**: OptionalLong with lag if available, empty otherwise\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalStateException`: Partition not assigned\n\n### 11.4 Metrics\n\n#### `metrics()`\n```java\nMap<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics()\n```\nReturns consumer metrics.\n\n**Metrics Include**:\n- Fetch latency (avg, max)\n- Records consumed (count, rate)\n- Bytes consumed\n- Bytes consumed per topic\n- Fetch size avg/max\n- Rebalance latency\n- Records lag (per partition)\n- Assigned partitions count\n\n**Usage**:\n```java\nMap<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics = consumer.metrics();\nmetrics.forEach((name, metric) -> {\n    System.out.println(name + \": \" + metric.metricValue());\n});\n```\n\n#### `clientInstanceId(Duration timeout)`\n```java\nUuid clientInstanceId(Duration timeout)\n```\nReturns unique client instance ID for telemetry.\n\n**Behavior**:\n- First call may block for cluster coordination\n- Subsequent calls return cached ID\n- Only available if telemetry enabled (`enable.metrics.push=true`)\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `IllegalStateException`: Telemetry not enabled\n\n---\n\n## 12. Common Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### 12.1 Basic Consumption Loop\n\n```java\npublic class SimpleConsumer {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        props.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        props.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n\n        try {\n            while (true) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    System.out.println(\"Offset: \" + record.offset() +\n                                     \", Key: \" + record.key() +\n                                     \", Value: \" + record.value());\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 12.2 Manual Offset Commit (At-Least-Once)\n\n```java\npublic class ManualCommitConsumer {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        props.put(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\"); // Disable auto-commit\n        props.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        props.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n\n        try {\n            while (true) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n                // Process records\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    processRecord(record);\n                }\n\n                // Commit only after all records processed\n                try {\n                    consumer.commitSync();\n                } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n                    logger.error(\"Commit failed; consumer likely fenced\", e);\n                    // Handle or break\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        // Process record; if throws, entire batch must be re-consumed\n        System.out.println(\"Processing: \" + record.value());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 12.3 Per-Partition Offset Control\n\n```java\npublic class PerPartitionCommitConsumer {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        props.put(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n        props.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        props.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n\n        try {\n            while (true) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n                // Process by partition\n                for (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n                    List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n\n                    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n                        processRecord(record);\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit offset for this partition\n                    long nextOffset = partitionRecords.isEmpty() ?\n                        consumer.position(partition) :\n                        partitionRecords.get(partitionRecords.size() - 1).offset() + 1;\n\n                    consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n                        partition,\n                        new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset)\n                    ));\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        System.out.println(\"Processing: \" + record.value());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 12.4 Rebalance Listener with External Offset Storage\n\n```java\npublic class ExternalOffsetStorageConsumer {\n    static class RebalanceListener implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n        private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n        private final OffsetStore store;\n\n        public RebalanceListener(KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer, OffsetStore store) {\n            this.consumer = consumer;\n            this.store = store;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Save offsets before revocation\n            for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n                try {\n                    long position = consumer.position(partition);\n                    store.saveOffset(partition, position);\n                } catch (IllegalStateException e) {\n                    // Partition not assigned (shouldn't happen)\n                    logger.warn(\"Position not available for \" + partition);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Restore offsets after assignment\n            for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n                Long savedOffset = store.getOffset(partition);\n                if (savedOffset != null) {\n                    consumer.seek(partition, savedOffset);\n                } else {\n                    // No saved offset; reset to earliest\n                    consumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singletonList(partition));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Don't save; partitions owned by others now\n            logger.warn(\"Lost partitions: \" + partitions);\n        }\n    }\n\n    static class OffsetStore {\n        // Implement offset persistence (e.g., database, file)\n        void saveOffset(TopicPartition partition, long offset) { }\n        Long getOffset(TopicPartition partition) { return null; }\n    }\n\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        props.put(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n        props.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        props.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        OffsetStore store = new OffsetStore();\n\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"), new RebalanceListener(consumer, store));\n\n        try {\n            while (true) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    processRecord(record);\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        System.out.println(\"Processing: \" + record.value());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 12.5 Graceful Shutdown with Wakeup\n\n```java\npublic class GracefulShutdownConsumer {\n    static class ConsumerWorker implements Runnable {\n        private final AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);\n        private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n        private final BlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue;\n\n        public ConsumerWorker(KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer,\n                            BlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue) {\n            this.consumer = consumer;\n            this.queue = queue;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void run() {\n            try {\n                consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n\n                while (!closed.get()) {\n                    try {\n                        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n                        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                            queue.put(record);\n                        }\n                    } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n                    }\n                }\n            } catch (WakeupException e) {\n                if (!closed.get()) {\n                    throw e; // Unexpected wakeup\n                }\n            } finally {\n                logger.info(\"Closing consumer\");\n                consumer.close();\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void shutdown() {\n            logger.info(\"Initiating shutdown\");\n            closed.set(true);\n            consumer.wakeup(); // Wake up from poll()\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        props.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        props.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        BlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue = new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(1000);\n\n        ConsumerWorker worker = new ConsumerWorker(consumer, queue);\n        Thread consumerThread = new Thread(worker);\n        consumerThread.start();\n\n        // Shutdown hook\n        Runtime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(worker::shutdown));\n\n        // Process from queue (separate thread)\n        ExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(5);\n        for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n            executor.execute(() -> {\n                try {\n                    while (true) {\n                        ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = queue.poll(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n                        if (record != null) {\n                            processRecord(record);\n                        }\n                    }\n                } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                    Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n                }\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        System.out.println(\"Processing: \" + record.value());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 12.6 Timestamp-Based Seeking\n\n```java\npublic class TimestampSeekingConsumer {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        props.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        props.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n\n        // Assign partitions manually for deterministic seeking\n        List<TopicPartition> partitions = new ArrayList<>();\n        List<PartitionInfo> infos = consumer.partitionsFor(\"my-topic\");\n        for (PartitionInfo info : infos) {\n            partitions.add(new TopicPartition(info.topic(), info.partition()));\n        }\n        consumer.assign(partitions);\n\n        // Seek to 1 hour ago\n        long oneHourAgoMillis = System.currentTimeMillis() - 3600000;\n        Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestamps = new HashMap<>();\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            timestamps.put(partition, oneHourAgoMillis);\n        }\n\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestamps);\n        for (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n            if (entry.getValue() != null) {\n                consumer.seek(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().offset());\n                System.out.println(\"Seeking \" + entry.getKey() + \" to offset \" + entry.getValue().offset());\n            } else {\n                // No records at that timestamp; seek to end\n                consumer.seekToEnd(Collections.singletonList(entry.getKey()));\n            }\n        }\n\n        try {\n            while (true) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    System.out.println(\"Offset: \" + record.offset() +\n                                     \", Timestamp: \" + record.timestamp() +\n                                     \", Value: \" + record.value());\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 12.7 Exactly-Once with Transactional Producer\n\n```java\npublic class ExactlyOnceWithTransactions {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        // Consumer configured for committed reads\n        Properties consumerProps = new Properties();\n        consumerProps.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        consumerProps.put(\"group.id\", \"consumer-group\");\n        consumerProps.put(\"isolation.level\", \"read_committed\"); // Only read committed messages\n        consumerProps.put(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n        consumerProps.put(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n        consumerProps.put(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n        // Producer configured for transactions\n        Properties producerProps = new Properties();\n        producerProps.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        producerProps.put(\"transactional.id\", \"producer-1\");\n        producerProps.put(\"key.serializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringSerializer\");\n        producerProps.put(\"value.serializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringSerializer\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(consumerProps);\n        KafkaProducer<String, String> producer = new KafkaProducer<>(producerProps);\n\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"input-topic\"));\n        producer.initTransactions();\n\n        try {\n            while (true) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n                producer.beginTransaction();\n                try {\n                    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                        String result = processRecord(record);\n                        producer.send(new ProducerRecord<>(\"output-topic\", result));\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit both transaction and offsets atomically\n                    producer.sendOffsetsToTransaction(\n                        buildOffsetMap(consumer, records),\n                        consumer.groupMetadata()\n                    );\n\n                    producer.commitTransaction();\n                } catch (Exception e) {\n                    producer.abortTransaction();\n                    logger.error(\"Transaction aborted\", e);\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n            producer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> buildOffsetMap(\n            KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer,\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records) {\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\n        for (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n            List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n            long nextOffset = partitionRecords.get(partitionRecords.size() - 1).offset() + 1;\n            offsets.put(partition, new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset));\n        }\n        return offsets;\n    }\n\n    private static String processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        // Transform record\n        return record.value().toUpperCase();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 13. Key Configuration Properties\n\n| Property | Default | Description |\n|----------|---------|-------------|\n| `bootstrap.servers` | \"\" | Broker addresses (comma-separated) |\n| `group.id` | \"\" | Consumer group ID |\n| `enable.auto.commit` | true | Auto-commit offsets |\n| `auto.commit.interval.ms` | 5000 | Auto-commit frequency |\n| `session.timeout.ms` | 10000 | Heartbeat timeout |\n| `max.poll.interval.ms` | 300000 | Max interval between polls |\n| `max.poll.records` | 500 | Max records per poll |\n| `fetch.max.wait.ms` | 500 | Max time broker waits for fetch |\n| `fetch.min.bytes` | 1 | Min bytes per fetch |\n| `fetch.max.bytes` | 52428800 | Max bytes per fetch |\n| `default.api.timeout.ms` | 60000 | Default timeout for API calls |\n| `isolation.level` | read_uncommitted | read_uncommitted or read_committed |\n| `key.deserializer` | (required) | Deserializer class for key |\n| `value.deserializer` | (required) | Deserializer class for value |\n| `partition.assignment.strategy` | RangeAssignor | Partition assignment strategy (comma-separated) |\n| `auto.offset.reset` | latest | earliest, latest, or none |\n\n---\n\n## 14. Performance Tuning Considerations\n\n### Throughput Optimization\n- Increase `fetch.max.bytes` to fetch more data per request\n- Increase `fetch.min.bytes` to wait longer for batches\n- Increase `max.poll.records` to get more records per poll\n- Use larger batch size in async processing (decouple consumption)\n\n### Latency Optimization\n- Decrease `fetch.max.wait.ms` for faster returns\n- Set `max.poll.records` to balance throughput/latency\n- Use `poll(Duration.ZERO)` to return immediately if data available\n\n### Resource Management\n- Tune `fetch.max.bytes` to balance memory and network\n- Monitor metrics for GC impact and memory pressure\n- Limit records buffered locally with pause/resume\n- Close consumer promptly to release connections\n\n### Rebalancing Performance\n- Increase `max.poll.interval.ms` if processing takes long\n- Use shorter `session.timeout.ms` for faster failure detection\n- Use cooperative rebalancing (modern default) to reduce stop-the-world\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe KafkaConsumer is a powerful, flexible API supporting diverse consumption patterns:\n\n1. **Group-managed consumption**: Automatic partition assignment with rebalancing\n2. **Manual assignment**: Direct partition control without coordination\n3. **Flexible offset management**: Automatic, manual sync, or asynchronous\n4. **External offset storage**: Full control via ConsumerRebalanceListener\n5. **Position control**: Seek, timestamp lookup, beginning/end offsets\n6. **Flow control**: Pause/resume for independent throughput management\n7. **Thread safety**: Single-threaded design with wakeup exception\n8. **Rich error handling**: Clear exceptions for different failure modes\n9. **Transactional semantics**: read_committed isolation for exactly-once\n10. **Metrics and monitoring**: Comprehensive observability\n\nDesign your consumption pattern around your durability requirements, processing model, and operational constraints.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1696,"cache_read_input_tokens":84731,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1696},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e1e96863-4dd1-457a-9aaf-69ff79f5231b","uuid":"7c88203b-9dab-4568-84c5-0d68918e24d4"}
